    <script type="text/javascript">
        function changeDay(dayType) {
            const tableElements = document.getElementsByClassName("diagram-table");
            Array.prototype.forEach.call(tableElements, function(element) {
                element.style.display ="none";
            })
            const target = document.getElementById("diagram-table-" + dayType);
            if (target && target.style) {
                target.style.display = "block";
            }

            const tabElements = document.getElementsByClassName("tab");
            Array.prototype.forEach.call(tabElements, function(tabElement) {
                tabElement.classList.remove("active");
            })
            const tabElement = document.getElementsByClassName("tab " + dayType);
            tabElement[0].classList.add('active');
        }

        function changeLineSelect(self) {
            let url = "";
            Array.prototype.forEach.call(self.children, function(element) {
                if (element.selected) {
                    url = element.value;
                }
            })
            location.href = url;
        }
    </script>
